\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{rlgl_8h_source_l00007}00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ that\ provides\ a\ pseudo-\/OpenGL\ 1.1\ immediate-\/mode\ style\ API\ (rlVertex,\ rlTranslate,\ rlRotate...)}}
